  slides (nav-forward/nav-back), Suspense reveals, crossfades вҖ” all declarative,
  all supported. This becomes the spine of the whole experience.
  в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ

  Now I'm going to launch a Workflow for Phase 2 вҖ” the design system foundation.
  This is where the maximal claymorphism layer + view-transition CSS +
  physics-based motion primitives get built in parallel by isolated agents.

в—Ҹ I need to be direct about a hard tradeoff before I invoke Workflow.

  The problem with fanning out Phase 2 into parallel worktree agents: Each agent
  would build a piece of the design system (claymorphism primitives,
  glassmorphism primitives, brutalism, view-transition CSS, motion primitives,
  icon set, etc.) in isolation. Then I'd have to reconcile them into one
  globals.css and one shared /components/ui/ вҖ” but design tokens are inherently
  coupled: agent A's --shadow-clay-lg must be the same value referenced by agent
  B's ClayPanel component. Parallel agents in worktrees would drift on the
  exact numbers.

  The right shape for the design system phase is sequential, in the main branch,
  with me authoring the coupled files myself. Parallelism pays off in Phase 4+
  (pages built on top of a locked design system).

  So I'm going to write Phase 2 directly here, not via Workflow, and reserve
  Workflow for the page-fanout phases (Landing scenes, Auth, Dashboard,
  Playground, Marketing pages, Settings) where each page is independent and can
  be built in its own worktree against the already-locked design system.

  Let me build the design system foundation now. Starting with the enhanced
  globals.css вҖ” claymorphism tokens, glassmorphism tokens, brutalism-warning
  tokens, view-transition pseudo-element CSS, physics motion tokens.

в—Ҹ Write(src/app/globals.css)
  вҺҝ В Added 601 lines, removed 34 lines

в—Ҹ вҳ… Insight в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
  Design decisions embedded above worth noting for the review:
  1. Clay shadows use dual light source + inset lines вҖ” the inset 0 1px 0 
  rgba(255,255,255,0.06) at the top and inset 0 -1px 0 rgba(0,0,0,0.35) at the
  bottom is what makes clay read as "pillowy" instead of "flat card with a drop
  shadow." The ladder scales both the outer shadows AND the inset intensity.
  2. Provider-glow variants (clay-aws/azure/gcp/ai) вҖ” this is what wires
  DESIGN_SYSTEM's "provider accents" into the tactile layer. Hovering an AWS
  node lights it orange; the same clay panel shape but the shadow tells you
  which cloud.
  3. View-transition CSS lives in globals.css, not per-page вҖ” because Next 16's
  <ViewTransition> uses class names in pseudo-element selectors. Every route can
  now request nav-fwd, nav-back, slide-up, morph by adding one prop.
  4. ::selection uses --bc-ai purple вҖ” small detail, but selection color is a
  signature moment users see hundreds of times. Purple ties selection to "AI
  intelligence" вҖ” subliminal reinforcement.
  в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ

  Now the primitive components. I'll build the claymorphic Button + Panel + Card
  primitives вҖ” the atoms every page uses.

  Read 2 files (ctrl+o to expand)

в—Ҹ Existing Button primitive is standard shadcn вҖ” I'll extend it with claymorphic
  variants (clay, clay-primary, clay-provider, glass, brut-warning) rather than
  rewrite it. That keeps every existing form field working while adding the new
  surface language.

в—Ҹ Write(src/components/ui/button.tsx)
  вҺҝ В Added 110 lines, removed 12 lines

вқҜ use react si instead of lucide icons 

в—Ҹ Understood вҖ” switching from lucide-react to react-icons (I'm reading "react
  si" as react-icons, which is the icon aggregator that bundles Simple Icons,
  Feather, Heroicons, Material, Font Awesome, etc вҖ” ~30 icon packs. That's a
  massive upgrade over lucide-react for the "most mesmerizing icons" bar you
  set. It solves the brand-icon problem too вҖ” react-icons/si gives AWS, Azure,
  GCP, GitHub, X, LinkedIn officially.)

в—Ҹ 17 files. react-icons@5.7.0 installed. Let me build a central icon barrel that
  maps every icon used to its react-icons equivalent вҖ” this way every file
  imports from @/components/icons and future swaps are one-file changes.

  вҳ… Insight в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
  Icon-pack strategy вҖ” reading each pack's identity into where it fits:
  - si (Simple Icons) вҖ” brand marks: GitHub, X, LinkedIn, AWS, Azure, GCP,
  Docker, Kubernetes, Terraform. Mono-glyph, one-color.
  - hi2 (Heroicons v2 outline) вҖ” primary UI actions: navigation, close, arrows,
  checkmarks. Tailwind's official pack вҖ” pairs well with our design language.
  - pi (Phosphor) вҖ” organic/decorative: sparkles, stars, orbits, cloud, cosmic.
  Best "mesmerizing" pack вҖ” has multiple weights
  (thin/light/regular/bold/duotone/fill).
  - rx (Radix Icons) вҖ” controls: caret, cross, dot-filled. Small, precise UI
  atoms.
  - fi (Feather) вҖ” fallbacks where lucide's exact glyph mattered (lucide was
  originally a fork of Feather).
  в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ

      131 +/**                                                           
      132 + * StaggerItem вҖ” child slot for <Stagger>. Uses fadeInUp varia
          +nts by default.                                               
      133 + * A no-op passthrough when reduced motion is on, so semantics
          + stay identical.                                              
      134 + */                                                           
      135 +export function StaggerItem({                                 
      136 +  children,                                                   
      137 +  ...props                                                    
      138 +}: DivProps & { children: ReactNode }) {                      
      139 +  const reduce = useReducedMotion();                          
      140 +  if (reduce) return <div {...(props as React.HTMLAttributes<H
          +TMLDivElement>)}>{children}</div>;                            
      141 +  return (                                                    
      142 +    <motion.div variants={fadeInUp} {...props}>               
      143 +      {children}                                              
      144 +    </motion.div>                                             
      145 +  );                                                          
      146 +}

      150  export { motion, useReducedMotion };
